<pics>None<//pics><username>Raymond Reyes</username><time>1540369818694</time>< Text>
Delicious and very authentic Mexican food.  Good portions and great taste/quality.  Same owners since the 90s and their product has been the proof of their sucess.  This is a go-to spot for locals.  Very friendly staff.  Too bad they are no longer a meat market, as their marinated "carne para asar" (flap steak) was the best I had ever bought.  While I was stationed at Camp Pendleton, their carne para asar was a staple at our weekend functions.  They've eliminated  the meat market and currently use the space to make fruit salads, smoothies,  ice cream, among many other delicious treats.  A must go spot for anyone craving some good Mexican cuisine in South OC.</Text>

I've rarely posted a negative review on a business because I try to be fair considering various circumstances. Not to mention, your customer service has to be absolutely terrible! Let me tell you, I will NEVER return to this place and will deter anyone who asks about it. The customer service was awful!!! Let's start by the phone call we made. It's a Monday night and my hubby and I just want to have a decent dinner. Ramen sounds amazing. We call to ask if they have outdoor seating and what the wait time is. The person on the receiving end is less than thrilled. No personality and acts annoyed by the phone call. We get there and it's a ghost town. They have one table outside and no clear instructions on whether you order inside or if someone will be greeting you outside. We walk in and granted, there are signs saying that masks are required, at which point my hubby realized he forgot his. There is no employee to be found and we just walked blindly through the oddly laid out "restaurant". We finally walk over to a place that looks like menus and a counter of sorts. There's an employee that's behind a partition with gaps and is on her phone. She doesn't greet us. My husband says "hi" to her first and she says "hi". Doesn't say, "can I take your order" or "can I help you". She just stands by the register staring at us. She then peeks around the partition type thing and asks my husband, "do you have a mask?" My husband replies, "no sorry, I forgot it". She says something like, "you need a mask". My hubby gets a little flustered and wants to leave at that point, but I tell him, "just tell me what you want and I'll order and pay". He's pointing at the menu and telling me what he wants and another lady appears out of nowhere and says to my husband, "you need to go outside!" Not "I'm sorry sir, but without a mask, I'm going to have to ask you to please step outside to talk about your order". No, she was extremely rude. There was NO reason for it and I'm shocked by the lack of care considering there was nobody there. They clearly need the business! Granted, had they been busy or even had ONE customer inside, I can understand the persistence, but NOT ONE OTHER customer was inside. The employees themselves were nowhere to be found! Plus, there was at least 15 + feet between us and the employee with a huge desk type thing in between us! It's almost comical how absolutely ridiculous these people acted. NEVER again will I visit this place!</text>

< text>
Ramen song is ok and getting better. Compared to the first time I went, opening week, they have done a lot to improve. The gyoza is phenomenal. The pork in the Tonkatsu doesn't have a lot of flavor and the broth isn't so flavorful that it makes up for it. But like I said it was a 3 star review the first time I came and now they are a 4 star, I fully expect them to improve to a 5 star ramen experience.
The restaurant itself is beautifully styled, and is always very clean. It's an interesting layout having been a former movie theater.
The staff is awesome and friendly and knowledgeable.
This place is worth a visit, even if it's a late night visit to "The Box Office" which is their late night offerings, purchased through the former box office window, which a really cool idea and convenient after a night of drinking.<//text>

< review>
First impression was good until I got the check.  For two people eating ramen, 1 appetizer and two sodas it was almost fifty dollars.  I would gladly pay for that if it was worth it, but the ramen was far from high quality.  As many reviewers mention they seem to not get the ramen right or at least on the same consistency.
The second time my girl friend and I went we waited more than twenty minutes without seeing our waitress again.  We were seated and brought a menu but nothing else happened.  We were told it was "slow" that evening with only two other tables.  After a few songs played I got the idea that something was off and to not bother to wait any longer.  We went to Wok in cafe instead and were seated, served, and eating within half the time.
Cons - Price is a little steep for mediocre ramen.  Only had pork or vegan style.  More selection would be nice. Menu is difficult to read if you don't speak Japanese, as the item is listed but not explained to what it is.  Bathrooms are upstairs and downstairs not handicap accessible.  Unless there are special ones not mentioned.  The hours of operation are split so make sure they are open before you go.
Pros- Its local.  Its secluded.  The decor is nice.  The guy that works as the waiter and manager (owner?) is very nice.  Food looks pretty.
I would consider returning or recommending to friends if the quality of the food increased or the price was lowered.< /review>

< Rating>
2<//Rating>
<Time>1572013208864< /Time>< Review>
The interior design and atmosphere is superb, as is the unique location in downtown Redlands. There is no designated parking lot, but the free city garage is across the street (accessed from Citrus at 5th) as well as free street parking. The employees all seemed friendly, however they were less than attentive with our large group on a busy night. As for the food, to put it bluntly it's not good. It LOOKS good with a beautiful presentation, but the flavors and textures were all wrong. The vegan ramen comes with kale noodles, which leads me to believe egg is used in the regular noodles instead of kansui (lye water). With a very bare menu to begin with, I see no reason to limit the vegan option even further. I tried bites of the vegan broth, yellow noodles, kale noodles, spicy edamame, and vegan gyoza. The yellow noodles felt doughy and the kale noodles were mushy. The broth was rather flavorless (like peppery hot water), as was the edamame. After reading the multitude of reviews complaining that everything was too salty, I feel like the cooks may have overcorrected and left us with nothing to taste. My Tokyo Mule cocktail was quite good though, if not terribly strong.</Review>

While not the absolute best ramen I've ever had, I'd say it was decent for what it was. If I have a strong hankering for ramen I'll usually make the trip to Grand terrace and go to Kaz ramen but seeing as this is a closer I'd go out of convenience. Broth was lacking. Needed a little more "umph". Of course it can't compare to the ramen shops in little Tokyo or Japan as I've had the luxury to enjoy ramen in both places, but for simple convenience and location of many local Redlands watering holes, it's a good place to grab a staple "comfort food". I will say I was pleasantly surprised with how good the gyoza was though. That very much tasted like the gyoza I had in Tokyo. Fried rice was tasty too with a drizzle of soy sauce of course. Only thing I wish they had was pickled ginger. Such a good addition to any ramen.<//review>

Atrocious excuse for ramen. Bland broth with noodles that look like they came out of a generic package from an Asian supermarket. Softboiled egg is not seasoned at all. Yakitori also terrible.

<Name>Walter Macalma< /Name>< review>
NFCU is a great bank for secondary savings, checking and primary loans. I've been a member for years and although I'm a saving only now I always found the experience at my home location a little archaic. Let me preface by stating I have Chase and had a brief stint with Wells and BofA, but kept both the Chase and NFCU throughout. The features they have on their ATM's the service they offer inside and the convenience is simply unmatched and to still deal with carbon copy deposit slips is stoneage. I get the fact that they cater the Military family, friends and DOD, etc. which run on a slightly different pay schedule and funds availability, but for the average Joe these features are appealing.

I have my business checking, savings, personal and secondary savings at Chase and a savings only deposit only savings at NFCU with a stipulation that all widthdrawls be done in person. I had a bad habit of moving monies around at whim that got me in some dire straits so my fix was in person width drawls only. It's worked great as my secondary savings and I highly suggest it. NFCU is great for car loans too, but the feeling and ambiance here is a bit like a prison. Everyone in line seems a little too jacked for my liking.< /review>

< review>
This is probably the most exclusive spa I have ever visited. The ambiance is warm and relaxing, with a scent of soothing fragrance in the air. I visited with my wife for a 90 minute deep tissue massage. This was my first visit to this spa. After being greeted by a friendly receptionist, we were offered tea and lead to a waiting lounge with dim lighting and relaxing music. We didn't mind, that we had to wait for a while, until our massage therapist introduced herself to us and offered us a foot soak.
Unfortunately for me, my therapist and I were matched up incorrectly. A mismatch, if you will. I usually ask for a stronger person to "get really in there", but failed to request that at booking. So the massage was not as satisfying as I had hoped for.
That can happen.
But, here is where excellent customer service comes in to play. Upon bringing my concern to the spa directors attention, I was matched up with a "stronger" therapist for a follow-up massage at no charge. And my trust in Serenity Spa was restored.
I often tend to rate a business by the ability to handle questions and concerns besides other things, of course.  And I must say, the spa directors actions impressed me. I will definitely come back again. Thank you!< /review>
